					</Grid.RowDefinitions>

					<TextBlock Style="{StaticResource ComputerNameFieldStyle}" />

					<TextBlock Style="{StaticResource PinCodeFieldStyle}" />

							adx:FocusHelper.FocusOnLoaded="True" />
			</StackPanel>

			<Grid Style="{StaticResource ApprovalStatusSectionPanelStyle}"
					ac:VisibilityHelper.VisibleWhenTrue="{Binding IsPendingOnlineApproval}"
					adx:VisibilityHelper.VisibleWhenTrue="{Binding IsPendingOnlineApproval}">
				<Grid.RowDefinitions>
					<RowDefinition Height="Auto" />
					<RowDefinition Height="Auto" />
				</Grid.RowDefinitions>

								 ac:RichTextBoxHelper.Section="{Binding [ApprovalStatusTextSection],Source={StaticResource LocaleResources}}"

						  adx:VisibilityHelper.VisibleWhenPopulated="{Binding Error}" />
			
			<!-- Buttons at bottom -->
			<Grid Style="{StaticResource BottomActionPanelStyle}">
				<Grid.ColumnDefinitions>
					<ColumnDefinition Width="Auto" />
					<ColumnDefinition Width="*" />

						  adx:VisibilityHelper.VisibleWhenTrue="{Binding IsPendingOnlineApproval}" />

				<StackPanel Style="{StaticResource ButtonPanelStyle}">
					<Button Style="{StaticResource ContinueWithReasonButtonStyle}"
							  ac:VisibilityHelper.HiddenWhenTrue="{Binding IsPendingApproval}"
							  adx:VisibilityHelper.HiddenWhenTrue="{Binding IsPendingApproval}"
							  adx:ButtonHelper.IsDefault="true" />
					<Button Style="{StaticResource ContinueWithGenerateOfflineApprovalButtonStyle}"
							  ac:VisibilityHelper.VisibleWhenTrue="{Binding IsPendingGenerateOfflineApproval}"
							  adx:VisibilityHelper.VisibleWhenTrue="{Binding IsPendingGenerateOfflineApproval}"
							  adx:ButtonHelper.IsDefault="true" />

							  ac:VisibilityHelper.VisibleWhenTrue="{Binding IsPendingOfflineApproval}"
							  adx:VisibilityHelper.VisibleWhenTrue="{Binding IsPendingOfflineApproval}"
							  adx:ButtonHelper.IsDefault="true" />
					<Button Style="{StaticResource ContinueButtonStyle}"
							  ac:VisibilityHelper.VisibleWhenTrue="{Binding IsRequestApproved}"
							  adx:VisibilityHelper.VisibleWhenTrue="{Binding IsRequestApproved}"
							  adx:ButtonHelper.IsDefault="true" />

	</StackPanel>
